What you do get with the WK7, though, is bass ‚Äì buttery, biscuit bass. If you like your music booming at you, there's no doubt you'll be a fan of this speaker. However, after coming straight from the richer Sonos Play:1 and the safer, softer sounds of the Echo Plus, hearing the vocals and bass go this deep sometimes gave the impression that the speaker was delivering muffled sound. Get a bit of Barry White on, friends, and let him melt inside the speaker.
